The real issue is that I'm including both the original and translated versions in the build, which causes the duplicate compilation.\n\nI should try removing the `.cu` files from the source list entirely and only include the `.cpp` files, letting the HIP layer handle the translation automatically.\n","time":{"start":1784347189340,"end":1784347192422}}}
